# Life Science 
Rhode Island’s life science sector is anchored by its extensive research capabilities with established institutions like Brown University, Bryant University, Rhode Island College and the University of Rhode Island among many others. With access to cutting-edge research, strong federal, state and local support and extensive funding opportunities, Rhode Island offers the ideal conditions for rapid growth.
Home to national leaders in neuroscience, oncology and the development of medical devices, the state has attracted more than $1 billion over the last ten years in NIH funding across our academic institutions, hospitals and labs. 
## How Is Rhode Island Advancing Life Science Innovation and Research? 
### State Health Lab and Private Lab Space 
Rhode Island’s new State Health Lab, alongside private lab space developed with Ancora Labs, enhances the state’s capacity for biomedical research and innovation. This expansion offers advanced facilities for companies in need of high-quality lab space and opportunities for collaboration.
### Rhode Island Life Science Hub 
The Rhode Island Life Science Hub serves as a central point for collaboration connecting academia, industry and government to drive growth in the life sciences. This initiative is designed to streamline partnerships, foster innovation and expand access to resources for biomedical companies. 
### Innovation Voucher Program 
The Innovation Voucher Program is part of Rhode Island Commerce’s Innovation Initiatives Portfolio created to support Rhode Island’s small businesses and entrepreneurs, including in key areas like medical technology and biomedical research. The Innovation Voucher funds strategic investments in local businesses that catalyze growth through research and development (R&D) and innovation.
Whether you’re looking to develop, research, innovate or scale a biotech venture, Rhode Island offers the infrastructure, resources and support to turn your vision into reality.
##  For more information: 
###  Get connected to a business engagement specialist today.
We're here to help. 
For More Information

# Site Selection
##   Development Districts 
The Rhode Island Commerce Corporation connects businesses with prime development opportunities throughout the state. 
 Learn More  
 !An aerial view of the 195 development district in Providence, RI. 
##   Foreign Trade Zone (FTZ) 
The Rhode Island Commerce Corporation manages three Foreign Trade Zones, helping companies cut costs and simplify their international trade operations. 
 Learn More  ")
 !A long exposure shot of Rhode Island T.F. Green International Airport at night. 
##   Opportunity Zones 
Opportunity Zones let investors reduce taxes by directing capital gains into specific communities through sustained business and property investments. 
 Learn More  
 !The Superman Building at dusk in Providence, RI. 
##   Property Search 
Rhode Island Commerce's commercial property search tool can help you browse local properties and development sites for sale. 
 Learn More  
 !Property Search

Rhode Island Commerce's Site Readiness Program provides funding to meet challenges faced by cities, towns, and developers, partnering for site improvements.

  * Preferences  4
Preference cookies enable a website to remember information that changes the way the website behaves or looks, like your preferred language or the region that you are in.
    * Airtable1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**internal/page_view** Stores data entered with a form so that when you return to the website you don't have to fill in the data again.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : Pixel Tracker
    * Simpleview1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**CFTOKEN** This cookie is used to determine which type of device the visitor is using, so the website can be properly formatted - This information is stored in the "CFID" cookie.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 30 years**Type** : HTTP Cookie
    * m.stripe.com1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**1** This cookie is used in conjunction with the payment window - The cookie is necessary for making secure transactions on the website. 
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
    * unpkg.com1
**plyr** Necessary for the implementation of video-content on the website.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Persistent**Type** : HTML Local Storage
  * Statistics  4
Statistic cookies help website owners to understand how visitors interact with websites by collecting and reporting information anonymously.
    * Simpleview1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**CFID** This cookie is used in context with the "Cftoken" cookie. The cookie stores a specific ID for the visitor and the visitor's device and browser. 
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 30 years**Type** : HTTP Cookie
    * Vimeo1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**vuid** Collects data on the user's visits to the website, such as which pages have been read.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 2 years**Type** : HTTP Cookie
    * app.powerbigov.us2
**ai_user** Used by Microsoft Application Insights software to collect statistical usage and telemetry information. The cookie stores a unique identifier to recognize users on returning visits over time.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 1 year**Type** : HTTP Cookie
**WFESessionId** Stores data on the time spent on the website and its sub-pages, during the current session. 
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTTP Cookie
  * Marketing  21
Marketing cookies are used to track visitors across websites. The intention is to display ads that are relevant and engaging for the individual user and thereby more valuable for publishers and third party advertisers.
    * Google2Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
Some of the data collected by this provider is for the purposes of personalization and measuring advertising effectiveness.
**_ga** Used to send data to Google Analytics about the visitor's device and behavior. Tracks the visitor across devices and marketing channels.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 2 years**Type** : HTTP Cookie
**_ga_#** Used to send data to Google Analytics about the visitor's device and behavior. Tracks the visitor across devices and marketing channels.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : 2 years**Type** : HTTP Cookie
    * Simpleview10Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**__Secure-YEC** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTTP Cookie
**LogsDatabaseV2:V#||LogsRequestsStore** Used to track user’s interaction with embedded content.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Persistent**Type** : IndexedDB
**YtIdbMeta#databases** Used to track user’s interaction with embedded content.
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Persistent**Type** : IndexedDB
**yt-remote-cast-available** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-cast-installed** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-connected-devices** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Persistent**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-device-id** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Persistent**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-fast-check-period** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-session-app** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
**yt-remote-session-name** Stores the user's video player preferences using embedded YouTube video
**Maximum Storage Duration** : Session**Type** : HTML Local Storage
    * Vimeo1Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window
**LOCAL_STORAGE_ID_VIMEO_PLAYER** Pending

    * YouTube8Learn more about this provider!opens in a new window

##  [ Your Success Is Our Mission ](https://commerceri.com/)
We provide business assistance, access to funding, workforce development and red tape reduction for enterprises ranging from startups to corporations. 
[ ![You Success Is Our Mission](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_732,q_65,w_499/v1/clients/rhodeisland/3_Steve_Kroodsma_Providence_Pedestrian_Bridge_a649b750-1765-45f2-b6ff-32c0e1565020.png) ](https://commerceri.com/)
## YOUR Business is OUR Business
Rhode Island Commerce is the state’s economic development agency focused on fostering business growth, attracting new investments, creating jobs, and strengthening the state’s economy. We provide businesses with the resources they need to land, grow and flourish in Rhode Island. Our suite of support includes grants, loans, tax incentives, regulatory streamlining and tailored business assistance.
[Learn More](https://commerceri.com/about-us/)
### Workforce quick facts
## 520k+
Employees in the Rhode Island Economy
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/workers.svg)
## 740K+
Rhode Islanders with a high school degree or higher
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/diploma.svg)
## #1
Rhode Island has the highest concentration of college students in the nation
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/chart.svg)
##  Why Rhode Island 
###  [ Free Business Resources for Emerging Technologies ](https://commerceri.com/emerging-technologies/)
Want to future-proof your Rhode Island business? Learn how AI and cybersecurity tools can transform your company—without breaking the bank. 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/emerging-technologies/ "Free Business Resources for Emerging Technologies")

###  [ Invention Incentive Program ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)
Rhode Island innovators: Get up to $5K for eligible expenses incurred when filing a patent. Ready to invent your next big idea? 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/ "Invention Incentive Program")
[ ![Invention Incentive Program](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/Sec_Liz_Tanner_Manufacturing_Day_FarmFresh_Commerce_HF_Oct24_151_0a15480f-5c74-4c9c-a831-cbaefecb61b3.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)
###  [ Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)
Rhode Island doesn't just welcome businesses—it supercharges them. From tax perks to personalized growth strategies, we're invested in your success. 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/ "Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline")
[ ![Aerial View of Cliff Walk](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_24877_jpeg_416d5e0c-15ac-4682-a221-2d4d8bde0ba0.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)
###  [ Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
Submit a proposal to design and build broadband infrastructure projects aimed at expanding high-speed internet access to unserved and underserved areas. 
[ Learn More  ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/ "Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects")
[ ![providence pedestrian bridge](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_19736_jpeg_9e5708e5-36e7-406f-abcb-9d7a76089ef2.jpg) ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
###  [ Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)
SupplyRI connects local suppliers to the needs of larger Rhode Island institutions, by facilitating partnerships, networking events and other opportunities. 
[ Learn More  ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/ "Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain")
[ ![Wavemaker Fellowship](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/WAVEMAKER_CARD_IMAGE_O_G_Studio_4_JPG_3__79806157-ec62-4855-9589-087991fbdc9f.jpg) ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)
###  [ Dive into the Future of Ocean Technology ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/)
Discover how the Ocean Tech Hub is turning Southeastern New England into a global powerhouse for undersea innovation, economic growth and national security. 
[ Learn More  ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/ "Dive into the Future of Ocean Technology")
[ ![ocean](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/Claiborne_Pell_Newport_Bridge_Newport_Newport_County_1__22b13d35-1e70-42d8-a2f0-a119d41180bf.jpg) ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/)

##  Your Success Is Our Mission
We provide business assistance, access to funding, workforce development and red tape reduction for enterprises ranging from startups to corporations. 
![You Success Is Our Mission](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_732,q_65,w_499/v1/clients/rhodeisland/3_Steve_Kroodsma_Providence_Pedestrian_Bridge_a649b750-1765-45f2-b6ff-32c0e1565020.png)
## YOUR Business is OUR Business
Rhode Island Commerce is the state’s economic development agency focused on fostering business growth, attracting new investments, creating jobs, and strengthening the state’s economy. We provide businesses with the resources they need to land, grow and flourish in Rhode Island. Our suite of support includes grants, loans, tax incentives, regulatory streamlining and tailored business assistance.
[Learn More](https://commerceri.com/about-us/)
### Workforce quick facts
## 520k+
Employees in the Rhode Island Economy
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/workers.svg)
## 740K+
Rhode Islanders with a high school degree or higher
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/diploma.svg)
## #1
Rhode Island has the highest concentration of college students in the nation
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/chart.svg)
##  Why Rhode Island 
###  [ Free Business Resources for Emerging Technologies ](https://commerceri.com/emerging-technologies/)
Want to future-proof your Rhode Island business? Learn how AI and cybersecurity tools can transform your company—without breaking the bank. 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/emerging-technologies/ "Free Business Resources for Emerging Technologies")
[ ![A cybersecurity demonstration.](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/temp_1d861b5b-9394-4c96-a45e-282042be58be.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/emerging-technologies/)
###  [ Invention Incentive Program ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)
Rhode Island innovators: Get up to $5K for eligible expenses incurred when filing a patent. Ready to invent your next big idea? 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/ "Invention Incentive Program")
[ ![Invention Incentive Program](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/Sec_Liz_Tanner_Manufacturing_Day_FarmFresh_Commerce_HF_Oct24_151_0a15480f-5c74-4c9c-a831-cbaefecb61b3.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)
###  [ Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)
Rhode Island doesn't just welcome businesses—it supercharges them. From tax perks to personalized growth strategies, we're invested in your success. 
[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/ "Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline")
[ ![Aerial View of Cliff Walk](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_24877_jpeg_416d5e0c-15ac-4682-a221-2d4d8bde0ba0.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)
###  [ Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
Submit a proposal to design and build broadband infrastructure projects aimed at expanding high-speed internet access to unserved and underserved areas. 
[ Learn More  ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/ "Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects")
[ ![providence pedestrian bridge](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_19736_jpeg_9e5708e5-36e7-406f-abcb-9d7a76089ef2.jpg) ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
###  [ Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)
SupplyRI connects local suppliers to the needs of larger Rhode Island institutions, by facilitating partnerships, networking events and other opportunities. 
[ Learn More  ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/ "Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain")
[ ![Wavemaker Fellowship](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/WAVEMAKER_CARD_IMAGE_O_G_Studio_4_JPG_3__79806157-ec62-4855-9589-087991fbdc9f.jpg) ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)

##  Your Success Is Our Mission
We provide business assistance, access to funding, workforce development and red tape reduction for enterprises ranging from startups to corporations. 
![You Success Is Our Mission](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_732,q_65,w_499/v1/clients/rhodeisland/3_Steve_Kroodsma_Providence_Pedestrian_Bridge_a649b750-1765-45f2-b6ff-32c0e1565020.png)
## YOUR Business is OUR Business
Rhode Island Commerce is the state’s economic development agency focused on fostering business growth, attracting new investments, creating jobs, and strengthening the state’s economy. We provide businesses with the resources they need to land, grow and flourish in Rhode Island. Our suite of support includes grants, loans, tax incentives, regulatory streamlining and tailored business assistance.
[Learn More](https://commerceri.com/about-us/)
### Workforce quick facts
## 520k+
Employees in the Rhode Island Economy
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/workers.svg)
## 740K+
Rhode Islanders with a high school degree or higher
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/diploma.svg)
## #1
Rhode Island has the highest concentration of college students in the nation
![](https://commerceri.com/includes/public/assets/shared/icons/chart.svg)

###  [ Invention Incentive Program ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)

[ ![Invention Incentive Program](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/Sec_Liz_Tanner_Manufacturing_Day_FarmFresh_Commerce_HF_Oct24_151_0a15480f-5c74-4c9c-a831-cbaefecb61b3.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/invention-incentive-program/)
###  [ Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)

[ Learn More  ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/ "Life in the RI: Where Culture Meets Coastline")
[ ![Aerial View of Cliff Walk](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_24877_jpeg_416d5e0c-15ac-4682-a221-2d4d8bde0ba0.jpg) ](https://commerceri.com/why-ri/)
###  [ Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
Submit a proposal to design and build broadband infrastructure projects aimed at expanding high-speed internet access to unserved and underserved areas. 
[ Learn More  ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/ "Design & Build Broadband Infrastructure Projects")
[ ![providence pedestrian bridge](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_19736_jpeg_9e5708e5-36e7-406f-abcb-9d7a76089ef2.jpg) ](https://connectri-ricom.hub.arcgis.com/)
###  [ Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)
SupplyRI connects local suppliers to the needs of larger Rhode Island institutions, by facilitating partnerships, networking events and other opportunities. 
[ Learn More  ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/ "Join Rhode Island's Local Supply Chain")
[ ![Wavemaker Fellowship](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/WAVEMAKER_CARD_IMAGE_O_G_Studio_4_JPG_3__79806157-ec62-4855-9589-087991fbdc9f.jpg) ](https://www.supplyrhodeisland.com/)
###  [ Dive into the Future of Ocean Technology ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/)
Discover how the Ocean Tech Hub is turning Southeastern New England into a global powerhouse for undersea innovation, economic growth and national security. 
[ Learn More  ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/ "Dive into the Future of Ocean Technology")
[ ![ocean](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_321,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/Claiborne_Pell_Newport_Bridge_Newport_Newport_County_1__22b13d35-1e70-42d8-a2f0-a119d41180bf.jpg) ](https://www.oceantechnologyhub.com/)
![Aerial view of a harbor](https://assets.simpleviewinc.com/simpleview/image/upload/c_fill,f_jpg,h_553,q_65,w_599/v1/clients/rhodeisland/140_3_13099_jpeg_07f3e32e-2e7c-479c-ac19-e99ba7f0ca5c.jpg)
